 profile SLA1_LOSS type cfm-synthetic-loss-measurement
  probe
   send burst every 60 seconds packet count 60 interval 1 seconds
   priority 1
  !
  schedule
   every 1 minutes for 1 minutes
  !
  statistics
   measure one-way-loss-sd
    buckets size 1 probes
    buckets archive 5
   !
   measure one-way-loss-ds
    buckets size 1 probes
    buckets archive 5
   !
  !
 !
 profile SLA2_ROUNDTRIP type cfm-delay-measurement
  probe
   send burst every 60 seconds packet count 60 interval 1 seconds
   priority 1
  !
  schedule
   every 1 minutes for 1 minutes
  !
  statistics
   measure round-trip-delay
    buckets size 1 probes
    buckets archive 2
   !
   measure round-trip-jitter
    buckets size 1 probes
    buckets archive 2
   !
  !
 !

    drop

    pass
  elseif (extcommunity rt matches-any comm_99_p1_permit) then
    drop
  elseif ((extcommunity rt matches-any comm_98_p1_permit) and (destination in pfx_IT_IN_2_p1_permit)) then
    pass
  elseif (extcommunity rt matches-any comm_98_p1_permit) then
    drop
  elseif ((extcommunity rt matches-any comm_97_p1_permit) and (destination in pfx_IT_IN_3_p1_permit)) then
    pass

    drop
  elseif ((extcommunity rt matches-any comm_96_p1_permit) and (destination in pfx_IT_IN_Gy_p1_permit)) then

    pass
  endif

  if (destination in TNB_MFFA_CustomerPrefix_Out) then
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy VRF_CD_SFW_DIAMETER_Export_RT
  if destination in CD_SFW_DIAMETER_Export_Pfx then
    set extcommunity rt (65535:66442) additive
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy VRF_CD_SFW_DIAMETER_Import_RT
  if (extcommunity rt matches-any SFW_DIAMETER_IMPORT_EXC) and (destination in EXC_SFW_DIAMETER_Import_Pfx) then
    pass
  elseif (extcommunity rt matches-any SFW_DIAMETER_IMPORT_EXC) then
    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy POI_TIME_SBC_SIP_Media_LP50_IN
  set local-preference 50
end-policy
!
route-policy VRF_VOBB_TMY_VRF_AVATAR_CP_EXT_EXPORT
  if destination in POI_TM_VOBB_TMY_CP_IN_Pfx then
    set extcommunity rt VRF_VOBB_TMY_CP_EXPORT_RT additive
  endif
end-policy

  additional-paths receive
  additional-paths send
  maximum-paths ibgp 2
  additional-paths selection route-policy RP_BGP_IPv4_PIC_EDGE
  nexthop resolution prefix-length minimum 32
  nexthop trigger-delay critical 0
  nexthop trigger-delay non-critical 0
  redistribute ospf 1 route-policy BGP_FROM_OSPF_1
 !
